info:Stayed in August 2022
info:Couples
info:16 Reviews
rating:4.5
posted:Posted August 19, 2022
msg:Not in the centre of town, but conveniently near a Wanda Plaza shopping centre and covid test site. The hotel looks and smells nice, and the executive room that we stayed in was really impressive. It was more a suite, with a full sofa/sitting area between the bedroom and bathroom. The  bedroom section had a really classy high ceiling look. Liked the room a lot. 

The executive lounge was not open separately, but we were able instead to enjoy the full dinner and breakfast buffets in the 1st floor restaurants. The selection and quality of the foods for both was very impressive and delicious, and we highly recommend them. 

This was a nice experience overall, and definitely worth the reasonable price.
